# 2.4 PsUser

## 2.4.1 General

**2.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `10974501`)

General
Description: Control of users

Used by: 5G-CP-RT

Addressing: [5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_58\_replaced([11176868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeQodvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

---

## 2.4.2 Procedures

### 2.4.2.1 User Setup

#### 2.4.2.1.0-2 User Setup Overview (ID: 10974523)

**2.4.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10974535`)

User Setup
Messages:

PsUser\_UserSetupReq/Resp

Purpose:

To setup a UE Context in 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Cell/Cell Group exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_188\_replaced([11188021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfIyPfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): SgNB Addition (3GPP NSA)

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_188\_replaced([11188021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfIyPfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): User and optionally SRB3 setup during SgNB Addition (3GPP NSA)

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_123\_replaced([11180017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BefSBvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): User and SRB1 setup in gNB-DU - Initial Access (3GPP SA)

[CNI-84537-A]5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1520\_replaced([11181581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BenNzfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Scell Addition in gNB-DU – for intra- and inter-gNB CA[End CNI-84537-A]

---

#### 2.4.2.1.0-3 User Setup Description (ID: 10974542)

**2.4.2.1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `12876735`)

User Setup
Message is used in below different scenarios:

SgNB addition (3GPP NSA)

* Used for preparing a new permanent UE context for SgNB addition.
* **DRBs are added and any DRB and UE specific parameters are provided.**
* **If the UE and gNB support NSA SRB3, the SRB3 configuration is stored and added.**

**Initial Access (3GPP SA)**

* Used to reconfigure "temporary UE" into "permanent UE".
* SRB1 is added and certain UE specific parameters can be provided

Periodic CSI and SR configuration parameters shall be included.

**For 5G-L2-PS actions required for PCMD see 5G\_L2\_1523\_replaced([11198349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29VgFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

If actAperCSI =  TRUE, aperiodic CSI configuration parameters shall be included.

**Measurement Gap configuration parameters can be included.**

New PUCCH configurations (format 0 & 2) to allow HARQ feedback from multiple UEs on same symbol shall be included.

If PsUser\_UserSetupReq message includes the ueAddCause set to “SCellAddition”, the following UE SCell information has to be included

- numDrbs and **drbAddReqPs[numDrbs], for DRB(s) which can be scheduled over SCell.**

- numOfCellConfiguration and **cellConfiguration [numOfCellConfiguration]**

o for the SCell to be added:

 perCsiRsResConfig(CSI-RS resource)

 perCsiReportConfig(periodic PUCCH resource) for SCell beam management and channel state feedback,

 pucchConfig: available PUCCH resource(F1 and F3 for HARQ-ACK according to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2920\_replaced([11310861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrTmu_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for CA UE PUCCH allocation in SCell 5G-L2-PS, and simultaneousHarqAckCsi is also part of pucchConfig

o for the P(S)Cell:

 perCsiReportConfig(periodic PUCCH resource) for P(S)Cell channel state feedback.

- ueCapability

- pdschConfig, including maxNumOfDlLayers, maxDataRateDl

For additional information please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2670.

Parameters maxNumOfDlLayers, maxDataRateDl have been moved from ueCapability structure to pdschConfig.

mcs-Table field added to puschConfig structure.

ulSchedTimeInterval moved from PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq to PsUser\_UserSetupReq**.**

actProactUlScheduling removed from PsCell\_CellGroupSetupReq.

Cell-level Proactive UL scheduling related operator configurable parameters added to PsCell\_CellSetupReq.

ulSchedTimeInterval moved from PsUser\_UserSetupReq to PsCell\_CellSetupReq**.**

ulProGrantType added to PsUser\_UserSetupReq to control proactive UL scheduling for each UE individually.

[CB008949-B]

pdschSupConfig structure is added to contain the PDSCH configurations which is supported to the greatest extent per feature activation status, reported UE capability and dedicated UE configuration at the time when PsUser\_UserSetupReq is sent. After PsUser\_UserSetupReq reception, L2-PS may send PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to trigger RRC Reconfiguration to the supported value provided by pdschSupConfig, and such PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd is not expected to be rejected or discarded by client for cell / UE configuration restriction reason.

[End CB008949-B]

---

#### 2.4.2.1.0-4 User Setup Message validation (ID: 10974577)

**2.4.2.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10974582`)

User Setup
Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserSetupResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the user was setup successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_387\_replaced([10974588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U8zv_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.1.0-5 User Setup Exceptions (ID: 10974588)

**2.4.2.1.0-5.0-8**  (ID: `10974639`)

User Setup
Expected Exceptions:

If at least one bearer can't be set up, 5G-L2-PS shall not set up any of the given bearers and send a PsUser\_UserSetupResp with "status" = NOK, "cause" field is not used.

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* ueIdDu IE is not valid or it already exists or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* all the requested bearers and resources were not allocated successfully.
* the crnti IE is already used by one existing UE

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause IE = Undefined, if:

* PsUser\_UserSetupReq indicates 5QI-1 bearer to be set up on a NSA cell

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause IE = InvalidParameter(2) if drbAddReqPs contains:

* default resource group which value is out of range
* default resource group for DL which was not configured if sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation is set to true
* default resource group for UL which was not configured if UL slice aware scheduler is active for a given cell (ulResourceGroupConfig was present in PsCell\_CellSetupReq)
* default resource group set to 0 if cell belongs to FR1
* [Before PR769857 ][CB008830-C] PsUser\_UserSetupReq indicates 5QI-1 bearer and DL DMRS is Type 2
* HighReliability bearer is requested in PsUser\_UserSetupReq and DL DMRS is Type 2

[End CB008830-C] [End PR769857 ]

Parameter Exceptions

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| ID | Invalid Values | Recovery Action | First Feature |
| 5G\_L2\_IF\_426\_replaced([10975509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFLvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) isFakeDrx | (isFakeDrx is present) AND ((actUlSlotAgg is FALSE) and (actDlSrsSubbandBm is FALSE)) AND (UE is on Pcell) | 1) Send a response message with status = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter. 2) Log an error. | CB008236-B |
| 5G\_L2\_IF\_389\_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PsUser\_UserSetupReq.ueAddCause   5G\_L2\_IF\_428\_replaced([10975561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBsNfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) pdschConfig.mcs-Table   5G\_L2\_IF\_430\_replaced([10975648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VCTQPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) puschConfig.mcs-Table | (pdschConfig.mcs-Table = 64QAM LowSE) OR (puschConfig.mcs-Table = 64QAM LowSE), then apart from the "ueAddCause" stated below, other "ueAddCause" is not supported.   - Handover - Intra DU Handover - Intra Cell Handover - SgNB Addition - Initial access SgNB addition - Initial NR-DC SNode addition - Resume Request - SCell addition | 1) Send a response message with status = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter. 2) Log an error. | CB008246-P   CB008246-Q   CB008246-K |

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

##### 2.4.2.1.1.0-2 PsUser_UserSetupReq CellConfigParam structure content (ID: 10974781)

**2.4.2.1.1.0-2.0-12**  (ID: `13456635`)

PsUser\_UserSetupReq
**CellConfigParam structure content**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

##### 2.4.2.1.1.0-14 PsUser_UserSetupReq perCsiRsResConfig structure content (ID: 10975404)

**2.4.2.1.1.0-14.0-4**  (ID: `12822322`)

PsUser\_UserSetupReq
**perCsiRsResConfig structure content**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| periodicity | ENUMERATED {sl5, sl10, sl20, sl40, sl80, sl160, sl320, sl640} | M | Periodicity (in slots) of the periodic CSI-RS transmission | 5GC000523-D |
| slotOffset | U16[0..639] | M | Offset (in slots) of the periodic CSI-RS transmission | 5GC000523-D |
| startingSymbolIndex | U8[0..13] | M | Symbol in the slot used to transmit CSI-RS. | 5GC000523-D |
| scramblingID | u16 [0..1023] | M | Set to Physical Cell ID of the corresponding serving cell | 5GC000523-D 5GC000720-C |
| density | ENUMERATED {dot5, one, three} | M | 38.211, § 7.4.1.5.3 | 5GC000523-D |
| densityDot5PrbLocation | ENUMERATED { evenPrbs, oddPrbs} | M |  | 5GC000523-D |
| startingPRB | U16[0..275-1] | M |  | 5GC000523-D |
| numOfPRBs | U16[24..275-1] | M |  | 5GC000523-D |
| locationConfig | U8[1..18] | M | Row number of table 7.4.1.5.2-1 in 38.211 Shall be set to 18 when 32 port CSI RS enable (act32PortCsiRs is True).  **[CB008577-B] For FDD beamforming (actBeamforming=True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80), only row 6 and row 18 are supported. [End CB008577-B]** | 5GC000523-D CB009459-B |
| frequencyLocationBitmap | U16 | M | As specified in 38.211 § 7.4.1.5.3 | 5GC000523-D |
| cdmSequenceIndex | U8[0..7] | M | Sequence index in CDM table (38.211, tables 7.4.1.5.2-2 to 7.4.1.5.2-5). CDM table depends on locationConfig. | 5GC000523-D |
| csiTransmitPower | For CPRI, s16 [-663, 0] For eCPRI, s16 [-903, 0] | M | Power of CSI-RS for feedback(Cell specific), see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2578. Optional.  Must be set when **locationConfig is 8 or 18**  Shall not be used when  locationConfig does not equal to  8 or 18. **[CB008577-B] For FDD beamforming (actBeamforming=True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80), L2PS will use this parameter for both locationConfig 6 (row6)and locationConfig 18 (row18).**   For FDD BF , refer [11269810: 5G-CP-RT shall calculate csiTransmitPower](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_To5y-PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [End CB008577-B] | 5GC002200-A CB009459-B |
| isExtendedPrecoding | TRUE, FALSE | M | Whether extended precoding mode is used. Valid for n1n2 = 4x1 setting only. | 5GC002200-B |

If dlMimoMode is ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4 , periodic CSI-RS resources are allocated for all UEs within the same serving cell for channel state feedback. Up to 3 CSI-RS resource sets are supported in cell level. If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks = 4, only set#1 is supported. **If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks = 6, only set#3 is supported. If act32PortCsiRs is true, only set#1 is supported.  [CB008577-B] If FDD BF (**actBeamforming= True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80), only set#1 and set#2 are configured.**[End CB008577-B]**

- CSI-RS resource set #1

o With one 8 port CSI-RS resource configured  when act32PortCsiRs is false [CB008577-B] or FDD beamforming (actBeamforming= True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80)[CB008577-B], or with one 32 port CSI-RS resource configured when act32PortCsiRs is true .

- CSI-RS resource set #2

o With two 8 port CSI-RS resource configured ,[CB008577-B] or with one 32 port CSI-RS resource for FDD beamforming (actBeamforming= True and cellTechnology=FDD and dlMimoMode=80) .[CB008577-B]

- CSI-RS resource set #3

o With four 8 port CSI-RS resource configured

For all the CSI-RS resources composing these 3 resource sets, the resource allocation of both time domain and frequency domain are statically determined in cell setup procedure (dynamic changing after cell setup is not supportted).

For backward compatibility consideration, periodic CSI-RS resource configuration for channel state feedback is still informed to L2-PS in user setup / user modification procedure.

For a certain UE, only 1 CSI-RS resource set is configured, and this 1 resource set could be any one of the 3 resource sets allocated in cell level (it is CPRT’s resonsibility to select a dedicated resource set for UE). If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is true and numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks = 6, CP-RT can select two or four resources from CSI-RS resource set#3, or CP-RT can select UE specific CSI-RS for UE.**[The CSI-RS resource set configured to a certain UE may change after user setup, e.g. from resource set #1 to resource set #3, or from resource set #3 to resource set #2, or from UE specific CSI-RS to resource set #3**.\*\*\*\*

If actCellCsiRsImTddNonBf is TRUE AND numOfSubSectors = 0, periodic CSI-RS resources are allocated for all UEs within the same serving cell for channel state feedback. One CSI-RS resource set is supported in cell level.

- CSI-RS resource set #1

o With one 2/4 port CSI-RS resource configured.

one Cell specific CSI-RS resource can be configured to UE.

If actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is TRUE AND numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks = 2, periodic CSI-RS resources are allocated for all UEs within the same serving cell for channel state feedback. One CSI-RS resource set is supported in cell level.

- CSI-RS resource set #1

o With one 4 port CSI-RS resource configured.

one Cell specific CSI-RS resource can be configured to UE.

Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3476 for several dedicated BWP per cell**.**

---

##### 2.4.2.1.1.0-15 PsUser_UserSetupReq aperiodicCsiConfiguration structure content (ID: 10975436)

**2.4.2.1.1.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `10975442`)

PsUser\_UserSetupReq
aperiodicCsiConfiguration structure content

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| aperCsiRsResConfig | structure |  | Defines the list of CSI-RS resources used for A-CSI reporting. See 5G\_L2\_IF\_422\_replaced([10975452](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFJvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | 5GC001817-A |
| servingBeamsBmp | U32 |  | Bitmap with the serving beams for which the CSI-AperiodicTriggerStateList is replicated. LSB means SSB-Index 0 Value zero means that AperiodicTriggerStateList has entries for each TCI-State, corresponding to each beam configured for the cell (bitmap shall be built locally by L2-PS) A non zero value means that CSI-AperiodicTriggerStateList is only configured with the TCI state associated to the beams having a corresponding bit set to “1” L2 PS shall consider that the entire triggerStateGrpPerSSBList is replicated for each configured TCI-State, as deduced from the above description. Example: \* 0x0000000A: aperiodic triggering states are configured for the TCI-states corresponding to the beam indexes 1 and 3 \* 0x0000001F: aperiodic triggering states are configured for the beams 0 ... 4. \* 0x00000000: aperiodic triggering states are configured for all the beams configured for the current serving cell.   [5GC001817-C] Set to 0 in FDD [End 5GC001817-C] | 5GC001817-A |
| numOfTriggerStatesGrpPerSSB | u8[0..63] |  | Number of trigger states groups per SSB-index in CSI-AperiodicTriggerStateList (CSI-AperiodicTriggerStateList is an RRC parameter sent to the UE). 1. [5GC001817-B] Each entry in triggerStateGrpPerSSBList is replicated for each serving cell that has a corresponding bit “1” in servCellsGrpBmp. The goal is to limit the number of CSI reports the UE is requested to transmit simultaneously (for the UEs that reports low CSI processing capabilities). [End 5GC001817-B] 2. [Before 5GC001817-B] Only 0 or 1 are supported [End 5GC001817-B] 3. [5GC001817-C] Only 0 or 1 entries are supported in FDD [End 5GC001817-C] | 4. 5GC001817-A |
| triggerStateGrpPerSSBList [numOfTriggerStatesGrpPerSSB] | structure |  | The common configuration for each of the trigger states group related to each SSB-index in CSI-AperiodicTriggerStateList. It makes it possible for L2-PS to derive the configuration for trigger states associated to any  SSB-index | 5GC001817-A |
| [Before 5GC001817-C] 1. >aperCsiRsResIndex 2. [5GC001817-C] 3. >csiRsResIndex 4. [End 5GC001817-C] | U8 [0…13] |  | in TDD, index in aperCsiRsResList of the serving cell corresponding to the i-th bit set to “1” in servCellsGrpBmp. 1. It corresponds to the CSI-RS resource mapped to the CSI-RS resource set selected for the trigger’s associated CSI-Report 2. The same index in aperCsiRsResList is mapped by all the CSI-Reports in a group (but notice that it corresponds to a resource defined in a different CC). 3. Only value 0 is supported (i.e. a single firstOFDMSymbolInTimeDomain for the CSI-RS resource is supported). 5. [5GC001817-C] in FDD, index in perCsiRsResConfig array. 6. Note1: in FDD, the same periodic CSI-RS resource is linked to both P-CSI and A-CSI reports for channel feedback. 7. Note2: the periodicity of the P-CSI-RS for channel feedback is increaed to SSB periodicity. 8. [End 5GC001817-C] | 9. 5GC001817-A |
| >aperiodicTriggeringOffset | U8 [0..4] |  | Slot offset (relative to the UL DCI slot) where the CSI-RS is transmitted, as configured in the CSI. 1. FR1 TDD: Set to 0. 2. FR2 TDD: Set to 2. 3. FR1 FDD: N/A. | 4. 5GC001817-A |
| >servCellsGrpBmp | U8 |  | Bitmap of the serving cells for which the above configuration pair (aperCsiRsResIndex, aperiodicTriggeringOffset) is replicated. 1. It should match the number of configured serving cell (this sentence could be revisited in the future). 2. The serving cells are mapped to the trigger state the same order they are configured, starting from LSB. LSB bit corresponds to PCell/PsCell 3. Supported value: 0b00000001 4. Additionally, In FR2, when CA is enabled, 0bxxxxxxxx is supported, where: \* x=1 for every serving cell configured to be reported with current trigger state. \* x=0 for every serving cell not configured for the UE to be reported with current trigger state.   Observations: \* A maximum of n LSB bits could be set to 1, where n is the number of serving cells configured for the UE. \* The i-th bit set to “1” in servCellsGrpBmp, counting from LSB, means that the i-th serving cell configured in UE’s context is considered for the selected trigger. | 5GC001817-B |
| [Before 5GC000885-E] betaOffsetACK-Index1 betaOffsetAckIndex1 [End 5GC000885-E] | U8 |  | Beta offset to be applied when up to 2 bits HARQ-ACK (see TS 38.213, clause 9.3) are received. When the field is absent the L2-PS applies the default value 11.   When the higher layer parameter betaOffset index for HARQ-ACK is absent, CP-RT shall fill the default value of 11.   [5GC000885-E] IE moved to new structure betaOffsetConfig of puschConfig in 5G\_L2\_IF\_430\_replaced([10975648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VCTQPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End 5GC000885-E] | 5GC001817-A |
| [Before 5GC000885-E] betaOffsetCSI-Part2-Index1 betaOffsetCsiPart2Index1 [End 5GC000885-E] | U8 |  | Beta offset to be applied when up to 11 bits of CSI part 2 bits (see TS 38.213, clause 9.3) are received. When the field is absent the L2-PS applies the default value 13   When the higher layer betaOffset index for CSI-Part2 is absent, CP-RT shall fill the default value of 13.   [5GC000885-E] IE moved to new structure betaOffsetConfig of puschConfig in 5G\_L2\_IF\_430\_replaced([10975648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VCTQPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End 5GC000885-E] | 5GC001817-A |

Corresponds to RRC IE: *ul-FullPowerTransmission-r16.* Note: Expected to be configured only if IE puschTransCoherence is set to nonCoherent (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_401\_replaced([10975032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_P9Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). |  |  |  |
| maxNumOfUlLayers | ENUMERATED { ulLayers1: 1; ulLayers2: 2} | M | Maximum number of UL Layers supported for the configured FR1 UL usable carrier. Note: The IE is meaningful for FR1 CC for SA/NSA, when puschConfig structure is present. The value should be as 5G\_L3\_5309\_replaced([11059142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BCWvcv_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))/5G\_L3\_5349\_replaced([11060530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BCc2Gf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)). |  | **CB006137-AA** |  |
| maxDataRateUl | u32 | M | UL max data rate as per TS 38.306 Chapter 4.1 The value is provided in kbps. The value of max Data rate is for the configured FR1 UL usable carrier for SA/NSA, not for the whole UE capability. Note: The IE is meaningful for FR1 CC when puschConfig structure is present. The value should be as 5G\_L3\_5309\_replaced([11059142](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BCWvcv_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg))/5G\_L3\_5349\_replaced([11060530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BCc2Gf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)). |  | **CB006137-AA** |  |
| minOfPmax | -30... 33 | O | The value equals to MIN (pMaxUeCapFr1, pMaxNROwnCell), and unit is dBm. pMaxUeCapFr1 means UE's PowerClass for the BandNR of a serving cell. pMaxNROwnCell is a NIDD parameter and means the maximum UL transmission power for a UE on a serving Cell. Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_1943\_replaced([11270388](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_To82QPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details. Only present if FR1 UL Scell is configurated. |  | **CB006137-BA** |  |
| [CB008148-A] actDCI01TpOn [End CB008148-A] | {TRUE, FALSE} | O | Indicates that DCI01 Tp On is activated. Based of flag actUlTransPreUsageEnh/DCI01\_TpOnOff\_StartTpOn; and UeCapabilities if present | [CB013707-B] L2-PS-Legacy: Not supported. L2-PS-Legacy shall ignore, see [13350878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JtAA4OvWEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw) for details. [End CB013707-B] | CB008148-A |  |

### 2.4.2.2 User Modify

#### 2.4.2.2.0-2 User Modify Overview (ID: 10975990)

**2.4.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10976003`)

User Modify
Messages:

PsUser\_UserModifyReq/Resp

Purpose:

To reconfigure UE parameters in 5G-L2-PS.

This service cannot be used to (re)configure bearer specific parameters.

This service supports add/remove SCells.

Precondition:

UE Context exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_192\_replaced([11188767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfNDofvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): NSA SgNB modification

[CB008140-BB] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1143\_replaced([11182271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Beq4I_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): SCell Release in Intra- and Inter-gNB CA [End CB008140-BB]

[CNI-84537-A]5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1520\_replaced([11181581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BenNzfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): SCell Addition Preparation in gNB-DU – for intra- and inter-gNB CA

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1750\_replaced([11182200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeqRGPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): SCell Change in gNB-DU – for intra- and inter-gNB CA[End CNI-84537-A]

---

#### 2.4.2.2.0-3 User Modify Description (ID: 10976009)

**2.4.2.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12876674`)

User Modify
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall reconfigure the given parameters of the UE Context.

Note that reconfiguring bearer specific parameters is not possible.

This message supports SCell addition, SCell deletion, SCell change and UE context modification (common and/or cell specific parameters).

In FR2 SA CA this message doesn’t support SCell deletion and SCell change.

For actions required for PCMD when reconfiguring cell configuration of an UE see 5G\_L2\_1523\_replaced([11198349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29VgFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For C-Plane optionally answering *PsUser\_BeamGroupChangeInd message, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_531\_replaced([10977540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VNSZvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). C-Plane can indicate that the message is not processed by setting* BeamGroupChangeAck = *FALSE or it is processed by setting* BeamGroupChangeAck = True or skipping this field. The values of the vector *beamGroup corresponds to the* PsUser\_BeamGroupChangeInd message. 5G-L2-PS shall process these two parameters as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2226 and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2227.**\***\*

Parameters maxNumOfDlLayers, maxDataRateDl have been moved from ueCapability structure to pdschConfig.

mcs-Table field added to puschConfig structure.

[CB008949-B]

pdschSupConfig structure is added to contain the PDSCH configurations which is supported to the greatest extent per feature activation status, reported UE capability and dedicated UE configuration at the time when PsUser\_UserModifyReq is sent. After PsUser\_UserModifyReq reception, L2-PS may send PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd to trigger RRC Reconfiguration to the supported value provided by pdschSupConfig, and such RRC Reconfiguration request is not expected to be rejected or discarded by client for cell / UE configuration restriction reason.

[End CB008949-B]

---

#### 2.4.2.2.0-4 User Modify Message validation (ID: 10976033)

**2.4.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10976036`)

User Modify
Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserModifyReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserModifyResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and the user was modified successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_452\_replaced([10976042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEIfvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.2.0-5 User Modify Exceptions (ID: 10976042)

**2.4.2.2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `10976061`)

User Modify
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object modification can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1811\_replaced([11375119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5tvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1812\_replaced([11375147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueL5v_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserModifyResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known or;
* crnti IE is not known or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not modified successfully.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from 5G-CP-RT, and that 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were modified by the 5G-L2-PS.

If PCell 5G-L2-PS receives the request with remoteSCellToRelease for non-existing inter-gNB CA/SCell relation, it shall not send PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq.

[CNI-101440]

If 5G-L2-PS receives the request with cookie IE it should be checked if a user (identified by ueIdDu) has PCMD cookie configured.

If cookie is already configured, 5G-L2-PS shall ignore new received value, not update cookie in internal storage and not trigger any actions related to PCMD context registration.

[End CNI-101440]

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

During F1AP: DL RRC MESSAGE TRANSFER over NR SRB with RRCResume(see 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_76808), this parameter is present and the state is "*inProgress".* |  | CNI-81991 |
| ueAddCause | ENUMERATED {InitialAccess: 0; RRCReEstablishment: 1; Handover: 2; UeAddWithoutRACH: 3; BeamChange: 4; BeamRecovery: 5; SgNbAddition: 6; IntraDuHandover: 7; IntraCellHandover: 8; SCellAddition: 9; InitialAccessSgnbAddition: 10; InitialAccessNrDcSnodeAddition: 11; ResumeRequest: 12} | O | During F1AP: DL RRC MESSAGE TRANSFER including RRCReestablishment message on SRB1, the *ueAddCause in L2 PS shall be updated into*RRC Re-est. **For SCell addition in ext-gNB (inter-gNB CA, see 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_60861) this IE shall be present and set to *SCellAddition.*   During F1AP: DL RRC MESSAGE TRANSFER over NR SRB with RRCResume(see 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_76808), the *ueAddCause in L2 PS shall be updated into*ResumeRequest.**   This parameter shall not be present in FR2 SA CA for SCell addition procedure. |  | 5GC000732-A |
| ueModifyCause | ENUM { RetainScellModWhileStepWiseScellAddOrUpgrade: 0; pcellModForScellUpgrade:1 MaxNumCause: 2 } | O | When this IE is present, the PsUser\_UserModifyReq is for retained SCell modification when another SCell is step-wise added  or Upgrade  to the UE. pcellModForScellUpgrade : Set only towards PCell having SCell upgrade from DL\_Only to DL+UL |  | CB006139-DA |
| cookie | 0…2^32-1 | O | PCMD cookie. If present, contains a valid value. IE provided during handling of RRC Reestablishment Request.   IE not used if UE already has cookie - provided during user setup phase. |  | CNI-101440 |
| perSrConfigChangeRollback | TRUE if SR Rollback is requested | O | Present only if the CP-RT decides to cancel the previously requested perSrConfig[] parameters. This parameter has to be used by CP-RT only in the second PsUser\_UserModifyReq during a ' back to back ' signalling of two PsUser\_UserModifyReq messages during a failue / roll back case initiated by CP-RT, in such case there will be no PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq after the second PsUser\_UserModifyReq. In a success scenario, PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq message will be used after the first PsUser\_UserModifyReq to complete the transaction. This procedure shall not be used in case only *payloadSizeSr have changed in previously requested*perSrConfig[] parameters, as it does not require RRC reconfiguration. **TRUE: CP-RT cancels the previously requested and L2-PS accepted reconfiguration of *perSrConfig[] parameters, initiated by a PsUser\_UserModifyReq message.  CP-RT also updates all the SR occasions in the *perSrConfig[] with configuration supposed to be used by L2-PS from this point onwards. Further L2-PS ends the transient phase, restores the mcs-table in downlink to the configured value (value configured for UE prior to SR Modification)*\*and responds to CP-RT with an ACK in PsUser\_UserModifyResp message.***\*   FALSE: Usage of the value FALSE is not allowed. L2-PS responds to CP-RT with a NACK in PsUser\_UserModifyResp message |  | PR619901 |
| ulCgConfigType2 | structure defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_4008\_replaced([10976380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VF9q_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | O | Present only when (NRCELL/actUlCgType2 is set to TRUE and CG type 2 configuration/deconfiguration is triggered), OR when (5G-CP-RT needs to indicate to 5G-L2-PS about CG deconfiguration, configuration cancellation, or deconfiguration cancellation (send ulCgConfigType2.ulCgConfig; see [11047581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BBZGK__KEe-D3seUwaI0tg) and [11320695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5G_WMgCfEfCESrsIqIgYfw)) irrespective of the NRCELL/actUlCgType2 setting).   Contains the CG type 2 configuration/deconfiguration information. |  | CB008124-A |
| nbrEnabledDrbScelllist[] | Structure defined in 5G\_L2\_IF\_5518\_replaced([10976500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VGkwfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | O | Present only when CB008227 is enabled in pcell and scell This is used to indicate Nbr enabled Drbs in each scell and triggered in context of s-cell addition/deletion and Drb addition on top of existing CA scenarios. ### 2.4.2.3 User Stop Scheduling

#### 2.4.2.3.0-2 User Stop Scheduling Overview (ID: 10976567)

**2.4.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10976579`)

User Stop Scheduling
Messages:

PsUser\_UserStopReq/Resp

Purpose:

To stop UE scheduling before the UE is actually released (by PsUser\_UserDeleteReq).

To stop UE scheduling on SCell before the SCell is actually released (by PsUser\_UserModifyReq)

Precondition:

Address distribution is done.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_190\_replaced([11188516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfLOhfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): SgNB Release

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_192\_replaced([11188767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfNDofvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): NSA SgNB modification

[CB008140-AD]5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1763\_replaced([11182767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BetUavvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): UE release[End CB008140-AD]

---

#### 2.4.2.3.0-3 User Stop Scheduling Description (ID: 10976585)

**2.4.2.3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `10976604`)

User Stop Scheduling
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling data on all bearers for the UE in order to protect scheduler from receiving L1 response messages after UE context deletion.

If **[CB008294-A]FR1**[End CB008294-A] CA user need to stop scheduling on the SCell(s), 5G-L2-PS shall only stop scheduling of the UE on the target SCell(s).\*\*\*\*

**[CB008294-A]In FR2 SA CA,** when **5G-L2-PS instance receives valid PsUser\_UserStopReq (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2569\_replaced([10976632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHy0fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the 5G-L2-PS instance shall stop scheduling data for all cells of the UE.**[End CB008294-A]***\****\*

If the UE Context does not exist, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the procedure is successful and return a response accordingly.

If PCell 5G-L2-PS receives the request with *cause=*interGnbCaUeRelease for non-existing inter-gNB CA/SCell relation, it shall consider the request as invalid.\*\*

---

#### 2.4.2.3.0-4 User Stop Scheduling Message validation (ID: 10976611)

**2.4.2.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10976617`)

User Stop Scheduling
Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserStopReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserStopResp message if the request message is valid, the user was identified and scheduling stopped successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_464\_replaced([10976622](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VHL2fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.3.0-5 User Stop Scheduling Exceptions (ID: 10976622)

**2.4.2.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10976626`)

User Stop Scheduling
Expected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-H]

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserStopResp also if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* scheduling was not stopped successfully.

[End 5GC000559-H]

Unexpected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-H]

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

[End 5GC000559-H]

---

### 2.4.2.4 User Delete

#### 2.4.2.4.0-2 User Delete Overview (ID: 10976718)

**2.4.2.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `10976735`)

User Delete
Messages:

PsUser\_UserDeleteReq/Resp

Purpose:

To delete a UE Context from 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

Address distribution is done.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_190\_replaced([11188516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfLOhfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): SgNB Release

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_140\_replaced([11182947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeuihPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): User Delete in L2RT in gNB-DU

[CNI-120470]

Internal event processing:

The L2-PS internal event dispatching of PsUser\_UserDeleteReq message could be either in a bundled manner or an unbundled manner:

* Unbundled event dispatching: upon PsUser\_UserDeleteReq message reception, L2-PS forwards it to needed sub-components immediately.
* Bundled event dispatching: L2-PS holds the received PsUser\_UserDeleteReq message(s) for short time period and forward them to needed sub-components within one single event when event boundig or forwarding criteria is satisfied.

Whether unbundled event dispatching or bundled event dispatching shall be applied is controlled by rdEnableUserDeleteInternalBundleMessage (5G\_L2\_18890\_replaced([11181753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27V7__vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For bundled event dispatching, event boundling or forwarding criteria is controlled by rdUserDeleteBundleWaitingTimer (5G\_L2\_18897\_replaced([11181764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27WjAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdUserDeleteBundleSize (5G\_L2\_18922\_replaced([11181774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27WjA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: internal event processing is not visible outside of L2-PS.

[End CNI-120470]

---

#### 2.4.2.4.0-3 User Delete Description (ID: 10976741)

**2.4.2.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `10976752`)

User Delete
**[Before CB008294-A]**

Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall delete the UE Context and all related resources, including all its bearers.

**[CB008294-A]**

Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserDeleteReq message, 5G-L2-PS instance shall:

 delete the UE Context;

 if 5G-L2-PS instance did not deleted resources during PsUser\_UserStopReq handling (see 5G\_L2\_8356\_replaced([11145223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23933_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then 5G-L2-PS instance shall delete all UE related resources, including bearers.

**[End CB008294-A]**

For actions required for PCMD see 5G\_L2\_1523\_replaced([11198349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29VgFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.4.0-4 User Delete Message validation (ID: 10976758)

**2.4.2.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `10976773`)

User Delete
Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserDeleteReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserDeleteResp message if the request message is valid **[CNI-120470] , the user was identified and deleted successfully** [End CNI-120470].\*\*\*\*

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_5364\_replaced([10976780](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VIZ6fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.4.0-5 User Delete Exceptions (ID: 10976780)

**2.4.2.4.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `10976794`)

User Delete
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserDeleteResp message also if

* ueIdDu IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;

[CNI-120470]

* the resources were not deleted successfully.

[End CNI-120470]

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

### 2.4.2.5 Bulk User Request

#### 2.4.2.5.0-2 Bulk User Request Overview (ID: 10976837)

**2.4.2.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10976849`)

Bulk User Request
**Messages:**

PsUser\_BulkUserReq/Resp

**Purpose:**

Bulk UE context clean-up after CPRT recovery.

**[CNI-113978] Bulk UE context clean-up for exception handling of CPRT.** [End CNI-113978]\*\*\*\*

To bulk stop UE scheduling before the UEs are released when type is stopScheduling.

To bulk UE context clean-up when type is deleteUser

**Precondition:**

Address distribution is done.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_2919\_replaced([11184000](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be0CKPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Bulk User Release after CP-RT recovery

**Relevant CP MSCs:**

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_94625 DU partial UE bulk delete

---

#### 2.4.2.5.0-3 Bulk User Request Description (ID: 10976855)

**2.4.2.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `10976867`)

Bulk User Request
When type is ‘stopScheduling‘:

Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling of all the UEs **[CNI-113978] listed in associatedUeList[] or all the UEs of the cell if no UE is listed** [End CNI-113978] and all its bearers in order to protect scheduler from receiving L1 response messages after bulk UE context deletion.\*\*\*\*

If the UE Contexts does not exist, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the procedure is successful and return a response accordingly.

When type is ‘deleteUser’:

5G-L2-PS shall delete the UE Context and all related resources, including all its bearers for all the UEs **[CNI-113978] listed in associatedUeList[] or all the UEs of the specified cell if associatedUeList[] is empty** [End CNI-113978] .\*\*\*\*

For actions required for PCMD see 5G\_L2\_1523\_replaced([11198349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29VgFPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1) Remote CA case will be taken care by CPRT in F1 reset procedure

2) In non-Remote CA Cells, all UE (PCell and SCell UEs) will be deleted.

---

#### 2.4.2.5.0-4 Bulk User Request Message validation (ID: 10976873)

**2.4.2.5.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `10976886`)

Bulk User Request
Upon reception of the PsUser\_BulkUserReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BulkUserResp message if the request message is valid, all the UEs [CNI-113978] listed in associatedUeList[] or all the UEs of the specified cell if associatedUeList[] is empty [End CNI-113978], are identified and scheduling is stopped or context is released based on the incoming type, successfully.

---

#### 2.4.2.5.0-5 Bulk User Request Concurrency handling (ID: 12813778)

**2.4.2.5.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12813781`)

Bulk User Request
Parallel message processing is not expected by 5G-L2-PS for below cases:

* between two PsUser\_BulkUserReq messages do not containing any associatedUeList[] array item. In other words, associatedUeList[] array is empty in both PsUser\_BulkUserReq messages.
* between two PsUser\_BulkUserReq messages containing associatedUeList[] array with same last ueIdDu setting. That is, when a new PsUser\_BulkUserReq message containing non-empty associatedUeList[] is received, it’s last associatedUeList[] array item’s ueIdDu equals to the last associatedUeList[] array item’s ueIdDu of any PsUser\_BulkUserReq message which is still under processing, i.e. whose PsUser\_BulkUserResp message is not sent out yet.

For all other cases, L2-PS shall support the parallel message processing.

**[PR805033] 5G-L2-PS shall support in parallel processing of PsUser\_BulkUserReq messages whose associatedUeList[] is not empty. Informatively, ueIdDu of the last associatedUeList[] item could be used to identify each bulk user request process inside 5G-L2-PS.** [End PR805033]\*\*\*\*

---

#### 2.4.2.5.0-6 Bulk User Request Exceptions (ID: 10976892)

**2.4.2.5.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `10976905`)

Bulk User Request
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

• the request message is not valid or;

• the resources were not deleted successfully.

[CNI-113978]

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BulkUserResp message as if UE is successfully deleted if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known (object is not identified) for any associatedUeList[] item.

[End CNI-113978]

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

### 2.4.2.6 User Suspend Scheduling

#### 2.4.2.6.0-2 User Suspend Scheduling Overview (ID: 10976953)

**2.4.2.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10976964`)

User Suspend Scheduling
Messages:

PsUser\_UserSuspendSchedulingReq/Resp

Purpose:

To suspend UE scheduling when

* Handover is started, or
* RRC connection re-establishment is triggered, or
* SgNB Release is started

Precondition:

UE Context exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_190\_replaced([11188516](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfLOhfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): NSA SgNB Release

[CB008140-GC] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1948\_replaced([11183193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BevwqfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): User Suspend Scheduling in intra- and inter-gNB CA [End CB008140-GC]

---

#### 2.4.2.6.0-3 User Suspend Scheduling Description (ID: 10976970)

**2.4.2.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10976976`)

User Suspend Scheduling
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall stop scheduling of the UE and its bearers. See the details for DL scheduling: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4208 and UL scheduling: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4823,  5G\_UP\_ALG\_4831.

---

#### 2.4.2.6.0-4 User Suspend Scheduling Message validation (ID: 10976983)

**2.4.2.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10976990`)

User Suspend Scheduling
Upon reception of the PsUser\_UserSuspendSchedulingReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserSuspendSchedulingResp message if the request message is valid, the user was identified and scheduling stopped successfully.

Note: messageResult IE shall not be used.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_480\_replaced([10976995](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VJoDfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.6.0-5 User Suspend Scheduling Exceptions (ID: 10976995)

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_UserSuspendSchedulingResp also if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* scheduling was not suspended successfully.

[CB008140-GC]If PCell 5G-L2-PS receives the request with cause HO\_with\_ExtScell for non-existing inter-gNB CA/SCell relation, it shall not send PsPeerCtrl\_ScellUeSchedulingReq.[End CB008140-GC]

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

### 2.4.2.8 Radio Bearer Setup

#### 2.4.2.8.0-2 Radio Bearer Setup Overview (ID: 10977160)

**2.4.2.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12772255`)

Radio Bearer Setup
Messages:

PsUser\_BearerSetupReq/Resp

Purpose:

[Before 5GC000795-B]

To add a radio bearer (SRB2 or DRB) for an UE.

Only one bearer can be added and this service cannot be used to (re)configure UE specific parameters.

[5GC000795-B]

To add radio bearers to a UE.

Multiple bearers can be added. This service cannot be used to (re)configure UE specific parameters.

Precondition:

UE Context exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

[5GC000795-B] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_146\_replaced([11184978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be46mvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Bearer Setup in gNB-DU

[5GC000752-A] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_146\_replaced([11184978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be46mvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Bearer Setup in gNB-DU

---

#### 2.4.2.8.0-3 Radio Bearer Setup Description (ID: 10977166)

**2.4.2.8.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12772257`)

Radio Bearer Setup
**[Before 5GC000795-B] Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall add the given bearer.**

**[5GC000795-B] Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall add the given bearers to the UE context and perform the initializations in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4552 and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10528.**

Note that reconfiguring UE specific parameters is not possible via this procedure.

---

#### 2.4.2.8.0-4 Radio Bearer Setup Message validation (ID: 10977173)

**2.4.2.8.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12772258`)

Radio Bearer Setup
Upon reception of the PsUser\_BearerSetupReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerSetupResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and all the requested bearer(s) were setup successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2615\_replaced([10977179](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VK2K_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.8.0-5 Radio Bearer Setup Exceptions (ID: 10977179)

**2.4.2.8.0-5.0-6**  (ID: `10977217`)

Radio Bearer Setup
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known (user does not exist) or;
* crnti IE is not known or;
* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources for all requested bearers were not allocated successfully.

If logicalChannelIdentity IE for any bearer is not valid or bearer with the same logicalChannelIdentity already exists or bearer setup failed because other reason:

* For PsUser\_BearerSetupReq sent to inter-gNB CA SCELL, 5G-L2-PS shall continue setup procedure and fill PsUser\_BearerSetupResp according to the requirement 5G\_L2\_9166\_replaced([11145654](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7JPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* For other cases If at least one bearer can't be set up, 5G-L2-PS shall not set up any of the given bearers and shall reply with PsUser\_BearerSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set an appropriate cause value.

For available cause values, see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If in case of failure, if 5G-L2-PS is not able to do a proper internal rollback for all sub-systems, and the state of the 5G-L2-PS is inconsistent, 5G-L2-PS shall indicate this in the response message, set status IE = "NotOk" and set the needForRollback IE = TRUE. This is to indicate that clean-up is expected from the 5G-CP-RT, and that the 5G-CP-RT should not presume that no resources were allocated by the 5G-L2-PS.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause IE = Undefined, if:

* PsUser\_BearerSetupReq indicates 5QI-1 bearer to be set up on a FR2 cell, or
* PsUser\_BearerSetupReq indicates 5QI-1 bearer to be set up on a NSA cell

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause IE = InvalidParameter(2) if drbAddReqPs contains:

* default resource group which value is out of range
* default resource group for DL which was not configured if sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation is set to true
* default resource group for UL which was not configured if UL slice aware scheduler is active for a given cell (ulResourceGroupConfig was present in PsCell\_CellSetupReq)
* default resource group set to 0 if cell belongs to FR1

[Before PR769857] [CB008830-C]

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerSetupResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause IE = InvalidParameter(2) if drbAddReqPs contains:

* 5QI-1 bearer and DL DMRS is Type 2
* HighReliability bearer and DL DMRS is Type 2

[End CB008830-C][ End  PR769857]

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

### 2.4.2.9 Radio Bearer Delete

#### 2.4.2.9.0-2 Radio Bearer Delete Overview (ID: 10977286)

**2.4.2.9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12772260`)

Radio Bearer Delete
Messages:

PsUser\_BearerDeleteReq/Resp

Purpose:

[Before 5GC000795-B]

To delete a radio bearer (DRB) of an UE.

Only one bearer per message can be deleted and this procedure cannot be used to (re)configure UE specific parameters.

[5GC000795-B]

To delete radio bearers of a UE.

Multiple bearers per message can be deleted. This procedure cannot be used to (re)configure UE specific parameters.

Precondition:

Address distribution is done.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

[Before 5GC000795-B] None.

[5GC000795-B] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_160\_replaced([11185498](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be794PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Bearer Delete in gNB-DU without User Delete

---

#### 2.4.2.9.0-3 Radio Bearer Delete Description (ID: 10977293)

**2.4.2.9.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13384444`)

Radio Bearer Delete
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall delete the given radio bearers of the UE.

Upon reception of the request, P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall also initiate the SCell deactivation procedure for [CB014119-C] each SCell (including ext-SCells and intra-SCells) of related [End CB014119-C] CA UE (ref. 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_311\_replaced([11195870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfxrYfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))) if drbScellDeletionInd is set to TRUE [CNI-157588-F] and SCell activation method is not blind.  
If SCell activation method is blind and PCell’s 5G-L2-PS receives the request with drbScellDeletionInd set to TRUE, then 5G-L2-PS shall:  
•    delete requested DRB(s) from related SCell(s),  
•    keep related SCell(s) activated, i.e. not proceed with SCell(s) deactivation procedure.  
[End CNI-157588-F]

If the bearer does not exist (when valid LCID [1…32] is given) or when the UE does not exist, 5G-L2-PS shall consider the procedure is successful and return a response.

Note that reconfiguring UE specific parameters is not possible via this procedure.

---

#### 2.4.2.9.0-4 Radio Bearer Delete Message validation (ID: 10977308)

**2.4.2.9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12772261`)

Radio Bearer Delete
Upon reception of the PsUser\_BearerDeleteReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerDeleteResp message if the request message is valid, the bearer(s) were identified and deleted successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_503\_replaced([10977314](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VMEQ_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.9.0-5 Radio Bearer Delete Exceptions (ID: 10977314)

**2.4.2.9.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12772262`)

Radio Bearer Delete
Expected Exceptions:

[5GC000559-G]

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object deletion can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1815\_replaced([11375190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgwfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1816\_replaced([11375218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueMgxPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_BearerDeleteResp message also if:

* ueIdDu IE, crnti IE or logicalChannelIdentity IE is not known (object is not identified).

5G-L2-PS shall not send response message if:

* the request message is not valid or;
* the resources were not deleted successfully.

[End 5GC000559-G]

Unexpected Exceptions:

[Before 5GC000795-B]

In case of unexpected exception (LCID out of range for example), no response message is returned.

[End 5GC000795-B]

[5GC000795-B] [Before 5GC000559-G]

In case of any other exception (other than listed in 5G\_L2\_IF\_501\_replaced([10977293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VLdPvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for at least one DRB, 5G-L2-PS shall not delete any of the given bearers and shall not send a response message.

[End 5GC000795-B] [End 5GC000559-G]

[5GC000559-G]

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

[End 5GC000559-G]

---

### 2.4.2.12 Random Access Indication

#### 2.4.2.12.0-2 Random Access Indication Overview (ID: 10977449)

**2.4.2.12.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12815207`)

Random Access Indication
Messages:

PsUser\_RandomAccessInd

Purpose:

[Before 5GC001094-A] To indicate to C-Plane successful contention free random access (CFRA). [End 5GC001094-A]

[5GC001094-A] To indicate to C-Plane both of the successful contention free random access (CFRA) or the contention based random access (CBRA).

* for CFRA, release the dedicated preamble allocated in the target cell and the 5G-L2-LO/PS/HI resource of the source cell.
* for CBRA, release the 5G-L2-LO/PS/HI resource of the source cell.

[End 5GC001094-A]

Precondition:

[Before 5GC001094-A]UE context exists and dedicated preamble is reserved. [End 5GC001094-A]

[5GC001094-A]

CFRA: UE context exists and dedicated preamble is reserved for target cell.

CBRA: UE context exists in the source cell.

[End 5GC001094-A]

Addressing:

The indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

[Before 5GC001094-A] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_184\_replaced([11187642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfG9CPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Contention free RA procedure. [End 5GC001094-A]

[5GC001094-A] 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_184\_replaced([11187642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfG9CPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Contention free RA procedure and 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_183\_replaced([11187006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfDSqfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  Contention based RA procedure. [End 5GC001094-A]

---

#### 2.4.2.12.0-3 Random Access Indication Description (ID: 10977455)

**2.4.2.12.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12815234`)

Random Access Indication
**[Before 5GC001094-A] 5G-L2-PS shall indicate to C-Plane successful contention free random access (CFRA). Indication shall be sent when the first PUSCH is correctly received after CFRA procedure. Based on the indication, 5G-CP-RT may release the dedicated preamble reserved for the CFRA.** [End 5GC001094-A]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC001094-A] 5G-L2-PS shall indicate to C-Plane successful contention free random access (CFRA) or the contention based random access (CBRA). Indication shall be sent when the first PUSCH is correctly received after CFRA or the CBRA procedure. Based on the indication, 5G-CP-RT may release the dedicated preamble allocated for target cell reserved for the CFRA and the old user context of 5G-L2-LO/PS/HI of the source cell (no dedicated preamble resource shall be released for CBRA case).**

**[End 5GC001094-A]**

**Note:** [Before 5GC001094-A] UE may select SSB with contention based resource (CBRA) instead of contention free resource (CFRA) even if CFRA resource was allocated by gNB. Also in this case, indication shall be sent by 5G-L2-PS when it stops monitoring CFRA resource in order to release the dedicated preamble. **[End 5GC001094-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[5GC001094-A] UE may select SSB with contention based resource (CBRA) instead of contention free resource (CFRA) even if CFRA resource was allocated by gNB. Also in this case, if no PUSCH CRC OK has been received, indication shall be sent by 5G-L2-PS when it stops monitoring CFRA resource in order to release the dedicated preamble, but CP-RT shall not release the old user context of 5G-L2-LO/PS/HI of the source cell.**

**[End 5GC001094-A]**

---

### 2.4.2.13 Radio Link Status Indication

#### 2.4.2.13.0-2 Radio Link Status Indication Overview (ID: 10977496)

**2.4.2.13.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12815313`)

Radio Link Status Indication
Messages:

PsUser\_RadioLinkStatusInd

Purpose:

To indicate to C-Plane the status of the radio link.

Precondition:

UE context is setup and radio link status detection is started in 5G-L2-PS.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_130\_replaced([11180086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5AfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Radio Link Status Indication

---

#### 2.4.2.13.0-3 Radio Link Status Indication Description (ID: 10977502)

**2.4.2.13.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12815315`)

Radio Link Status Indication
5G-L2-PS shall send an indication of radio link status to C-Plane. See [5G\_L2\_IF\_5843\_replaced([10977515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VNSYvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))]

If 5G-L2-PS detects RLF, it sends "RLF detected" indication to C-Plane. See [5G\_UP\_ALG\_3350].

If, after sending "RLF detected" indication to C-Plane, 5G-L2-PS detects that radio link is active, it cancels RLF indication by sending "RLF not detected" indication to C-Plane. See [5G\_UP\_ALG\_3352].

RLF cause (DL HARQ or BSI/CSI) shall be indicated in the message.

**[5GC000478-D]**

Note: DTX detection of CSI reports will be possible with **[5GC000523-D]**

---

[5GC002184-E]

No exception handling in 5G-L2-PS for PsUser\_RadioLinkStatusInd message. The receiver/client of the message checks the validity where applicable.

[End 5GC002184-E]

Expected Exceptions:

None.

Unexpected Exceptions:

None.

| ueRlStatus | 0 = rlf\_off 1 = rlf\_dl\_harq 2 = rlf\_bsi\_csi 3 = bad\_ul\_radio **[Before 04742201][PR807896]** 4= ho\_cr\_failure **[End PR807896][End 04742201]** | M | 0 = RLF indication cleared (RLF not detected) 1 = RLF detected due to DL HARQ 2 = RLF detected due to BSI/CSI 3 = detection of bad UL radio conditions (5G\_UP\_ALG\_24965) **[Before 04742201][PR807896]** 4 = Contention Resolution timeout - intra-DU, inter-DU, and inter-gNB cases (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3441) **[End PR807896] [End 04742201]** | 5GC000478-A |
