### 2.4.2.14 Beam Group Change Indication

#### 2.4.2.14.0-2 Beam Group Change Indication Overview (ID: 10977552)

**2.4.2.14.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10977564`)

Beam Group Change Indication
Messages:

PsUser\_BeamGroupChangeInd

Purpose:

To indicate to C-Plane the beam group- or target beam change to be RRC re-configured.

Precondition:

UE context is setup.

[PR585488, PR582875] rrmBeamformingType = analogBf [End PR585488, PR582875]  or ([PR585488, PR582875] rrmBeamformingType = digitalBf, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1886 [End PR585488, PR582875] : and actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE), in CellSetup message 5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_UP\_ALG\_2233 and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2234: Beam Group Change Indication

---

#### 2.4.2.14.0-3 Beam Group Change Indication Description (ID: 10977571)

**2.4.2.14.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12815323`)

Beam Group Change Indication
5G-L2-PS shall send an indication of beam group- or target beam change to C-Plane.

If 5G-L2-PS detects beam change [5G\_UP\_ALG\_2006], L2-PS shall indication to C-Plane as in [5G\_UP\_ALG\_2220].

---

#### 2.4.2.14.0-4 Beam Group Change Indication PsUser_BeamGroupChangeInd (ID: 10977576)

**2.4.2.14.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12815324`)

Beam Group Change Indication
**PsUser\_BeamGroupChangeInd message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| ueIdDu | 0…2^32-1 | M |  | FGCR-3077 |
| beamGroup[size] | size{16} | M | vector of SSB-indices defining the beam group. | FGCR-3077 |
| targetSsbBeam | 0..63 | M | SSB-index of target beam | FGCR-3077 |

**NOTE: beamId = SSB-Index as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2227\_replaced([11113653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpcuZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). SSB-Index = SSBRI that is SSB Resource Indicator as reported by the UE, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1999\_replaced([11112098](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpS9avvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if first consecutive SSB-Indices are used.**

**NOTE: If CA in FR1 is introduced, the message should be extended by the field *nrCellIdentity (0...2^36-1), that is a cell id (unique within all PLMNs associated with the cell), since different beams at a time apply to different cells. Then in FR2, PCell Id should still trigger RRC re-configuration of beam (group) for all cells.***

---

### 2.4.2.15 User Reconfiguration Required

#### 2.4.2.15.0-2 User Reconfiguration Required Overview (ID: 12782309)

**2.4.2.15.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10977595`)

User Reconfiguration Required
Messages:

PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd/PsUser\_UserModifyReq/PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq

Purpose:

To indicate to C-Plane that  a UE reconfiguration is required.

Precondition:

UE context is setup.

Addressing:

The PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

The PsUser\_UserModifyReq is sent to the PsUser address

The PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq is sent to the PsUser address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_132\_replaced([11180104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bef5A_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): User reconfiguration required Indication

---

#### 2.4.2.15.0-3 User Reconfiguration Required Description (ID: 12782316)

**2.4.2.15.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12782322`)

User Reconfiguration Required
5G-L2-PS shall send an indication of user reconfiguration required to C-Plane and shall expect for completion indication.

C-Plane indicates acceptance of starting the UE reconfiguration sending the message PsUser\_UserModifyReq with :

nrofSrsPortsChangeAck parameter value "true" (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_453\_replaced([10976074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VEvgvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Completion indication comes with PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq indication message (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_2575\_replaced([10977732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VOghfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for message definition)

If 5G-L2-PS detects a reconfiguration is required, it sends "User Reconfiguration Required" indication to C-Plane (see [5G\_L2\_IF\_541\_replaced([10977614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VN5cvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for message definition).

L2-PS detects a reconfiguration is required when:

* an UE has "adaptive number of SRS ports" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3216) and the rank selection for the next initial transmissions changes according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3224 algorithm (see 5G\_L2\_656\_replaced([11164313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25sWIvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[04949764] Within the whole DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion procedure specified by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29060\_replaced([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2-PS shall abort PsUsr\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd sending to avoid new PsUser\_UserModifyReq triggering of CPRT. Rational: L2-PS could not handle new PsUser\_UserModifyReq well after MAC Layer Monitoring is started and not ended ([11153872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspMVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End 04949764]

---

#### 2.4.2.15.0-5 User Reconfiguration Required Exceptions (ID: 12782319)

**2.4.2.15.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12982586`)

User Reconfiguration Required
**Expected Exceptions:**

For the specific handling of the exceptions when the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure is used for the number of SRS ports reconfiguration, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3260.

[Before PR867429]

[CB012631-SR-D]For the specific handling of the exceptions when the "User Reconfiguration Required" procedure is used for the sssgReconfigurationInd, see [12798424: User Reconfiguration required for sparse SSSG](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Hr064Jj2EfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).[End CB012631-SR-D]

[End PR867429]

For exceptions when the PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq message is received, refer to 5G\_L2\_IF\_547\_replaced([10977726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VOghPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.15.0-6 User Reconfiguration Required PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd (ID: 10977614)

**2.4.2.15.0-6.0-8**  (ID: `12740349`)

User Reconfiguration Required
PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| ueIdDu | 0…2^32-1 | M |  | 5GC002226-A |
| nrCellIdentity | 0...2^36-1 | M | Cell Identity | CB006137-AC |
| nrOfSrsPorts | ENUM { notApplicable, port1, ports2} | M | NotApplicable: This indicates that this IE "nrOfSrsPorts" is ignored.   port1 : This indicates that L2-PS requires for User reconfiguration with number of SRS Ports port1   ports2 : This indicates that L2-PS requires for User reconfiguration with number of SRS Ports ports2 | 5GC002226-A |
| transformPrecoderInd | ENUM { notApplicable, enabled, disabled} | M | 'NotApplicable': This indicates that this IE is ignored 'enabled' : This indicates that L2-PS requires User reconfiguration with Transform Precoder enabled 'diabled' : This indicates that L2-PS requires User reconfiguration with Transform Precoder disabled | 5GC000545-B |
| tasSrsResourceInd | ENUM { notApplicable, wideband, subband} | M | NotApplicable: This indicates that this IE " tasSrsResourceInd " is ignored. wideband: This indicates that L2-PS requires reconfiguration for this UE/User to wideband TAS SRS resource subband: This indicates that L2-PS requires reconfiguration for this UE/User to subband TAS SRS resource | CB008322-B |
| puschTimeDomainAllocationList[] | structure [0..15] | M | See (12801792) | CNI-134949-A |
| puschTimeDomainAllocationListR16[] | structure [0..63] |  | See (12801793) | CNI-134949-A |
| noAddDlDmrsInd | ENUM { notApplicable, config, release} | M | NotApplicable: This indicates that this IE " oneDlDmrsInd " is ignored. config: This indicates that L2-PS requires reconfiguration for this UE/User to no addtional DL DMRS release: This indicates that L2-PS requires reconfiguration for this UE/User to additional DL DMRS.   5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_5645\_replaced([11180260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BeggGfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is the message flow for "No Additional Dl Dmrs" reconfiguration initiated user reconfiguration procedure. | CB011117-E |
| slotAggregationInd | ENUM { notApplicable, enabled, disabled} | M | 'NotApplicable': This indicates that this IE is ignored 'enabled' : This indicates that L2-PS requires User reconfiguration with Slot Aggregation enabled 'diabled' : This indicates that L2-PS requires User reconfiguration with Slot Aggregation disabled | CB009849-A |
| [CB011022-A] dlMcsTableChangeInd [End CB011022-A] | ENUM{ notApplicabe, qam64, qam256, [CB008949-B] qam1024 [End CB008949-B]} | M | 'notApplicable': this IE has to be ignored; 'qam64': L2-PS requires to reconfigure the DL MCS table to qam64;  'qam256': L2-PS requires to reconfigure the DL MCS table to qam256; [CB008949-B]  'qam1024': L2-PS requires to reconfigure the DL MCS table to qam1024; [End CB008949-B] | CB011022-A |
| [CB011022-B] dlDmrsTypeChangeInd [End CB011022-B] | ENUM{ notApplicable, type1, type2} | M | 'notApplicable': this IE has to be ignored; 'type1': L2-PS requires to change the DL DMRS type to Type1;  'type2': L2-PS requires to change the DL DMRS type to Type2; | CB011022-B |
| [Before PR867429] sssgReconfigurationInd [End PR867429] | structure | O | It is present when L2-PS requires to reconfigure sparse SSSG after cell SSSG parameter changed. | CB012631-SR-D |
| [Before PR867429] >sparseSSGroupIndex [End PR867429] | same index with  [10975890](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VDhY_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) | O | old SS index, It is present when L2-PS require CP-RT reuse this index. reserved for further use. L2-PS don't fill it currently. CP-RT reuse or re-allocation SS index by checking if there is SS change per this UE. | CB012631-SR-D |

Note: one only and only one \*Ind IE could be set to value other than 'notApplicable' within each PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd message. e.g. if nrOfSrsPortsInd IE is set to 'port1', transformPrecoderInd  (and also all other ..Ind IEs added in the future) must be set to 'notApplicable'.

[CB011022-B] [12483265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_pPSrwA-UEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) requires that, when possible, the DL MCS Table and DL DMRS type are reconfigured within the same RRC procedure. In order to fulfill this both "dlMcsTableChangeInd" and "dlDmrsTypeChangeInd" must be set to a value different from 'notApplicable' within the same PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd. Since for this joint mcs-table/dmrs-type reconfiguration no issues have been identified, both at system level and design level, it has been decided to overrule the limitation expressed by the note above, also considering that no rationale has been provided for that. [End CB011022-B]

If one Ind IE is set to value other than 'notApplicable' and might cause DCI conflict, then puschTdraConfigSet shall be filled. [CB011022-A] both a reconfiguration of the DL MCS Table (dlMcsTableChangeInd != 'notApplicable') or of the PDSCH DMRS Type (dlDmrsTypeChangeInd != 'notApplicable') don't affect the size of DCI\_01 and therefore don't require to fill puschTdraConfigSet. [End CB011022-A]

---

### 2.4.2.16 RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication

#### 2.4.2.16.0-2 RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication Overview (ID: 10977678)

**2.4.2.16.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `10977689`)

RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication
Messages:

PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq

Purpose:

To send an UE RRC Reconfigure Complete indication to 5G-L2-PS.

Precondition:

While CP-CU receives a RRC Reconfigure Complete message from UE, it shall send a message to notify CP-DU.

[CNI-134375-O]

Note: When 5G-CP-RT receives F1AP: Ue Context Modification Request message [5G\_CP\_IF\_NTW\_1187], it shall send (or not send) PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq, as specified in 5G\_L3\_2904\_replaced([11028193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_A_zKtP_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg)).

[End CNI-134375-O]

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

No response message is requested.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_134\_replaced([11180431](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BehHLvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): RRC Reconfiguration complete indication in User Modify

---

#### 2.4.2.16.0-3 RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication Description (ID: 10977696)

**2.4.2.16.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `13423169`)

RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication
Upon reception of the request with ulConfigurationMode is anything other than NotApplicable, 5G-L2-PS shall update UE DRX status according to the value of ulConfigurationMode UE RRC Reconfiguration Complete message.

5G-L2-PS will release measurement gap according to RRC Reconfiguration Complete message context if PsUser\_UserModifyReq indicating MG release has been received before.

While L2-PS receives a PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq from CP-RT with ulConfigurationMode anything other than NotApplicable, then L2-PS shall update the UlSplit\_workmode to the LTEOnly or NR state according to this value. Refer more to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3372.

Upon reception of the request with *beamGroup or* targetSsbBeam is anything other than NotApplicable, 5G-L2-PS shall conduct beam change as in [5G\_UP\_ALG\_2220] according to the values of the RRC Reconfiguration Complete message. The parameter *beamGroup or* targetSsbBeam shall be present in the in the message if C-Plane is responding a *BeamGroupChangeInd message 5G\_L2\_IF\_531\_replaced([10977540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VNSZvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*\*\*

**NOTE: Only applicable if rrmBeamformingType = analogBf: AnalogBF or if (rrmBeamformingType = digitalBf, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1886: DigitalBF and *actRrcReconfigAtBeamSwitch = TRUE), in CellSetup message 5G\_L2\_IF\_61\_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***

Upon reception of the request for CA UE with IE **drbScellAdditionInd set to TRUE, the P(S)Cell 5G-L2-PS shall initiate the SCell activation procedure (ref. 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_290\_replaced([11195606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bfv2PfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if Blind activation mode.**

Note 1: CP-RT sets the IE **drbScellAdditionInd to TRUE if the non-GBR DRB(s) in the corresponding RRC CellGroupConfig is(are) the first being mapped on the remote SCell which had no supporting DRB.  
[CNI-157588-F]Note 2: If SCell activation method is not blind (e.g. buffer based activation), then the reception of PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq message is not a trigger of Scell activation, as described in [11195650](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfwdQfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ).  
[End CNI-157588-F]**

In reestablishment case:

RRCReconfigurationComplete message is used to trigger Bandwidth part change from intial Bandwidth part to dedicated Bandwidth part.

In ResumeRequest1(5G\_L3\_FLOW\_70577) case:

RRCReconfigurationComplete message is used to trigger Bandwidth part change from intial Bandwidth part to dedicated Bandwidth part in resume complete scenario.

---

#### 2.4.2.16.0-4 RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication Message validation (ID: 10977721)

**2.4.2.16.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12815325`)

RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication
Upon reception of the PsUser\_RrcReconfCompletedReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_547\_replaced([10977726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VOghPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.16.0-5 RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication Exceptions (ID: 10977726)

**2.4.2.16.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12815326`)

RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication
[5GC002184-E]

Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall discard the message if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known or;
* crnti IE is not known or;
* the request message is not valid.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall discard the message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

[End 5GC002184-E]

---

RRC Reconfiguration Complete indication

| p0 | -202…24 | O | Present when NRCELL/actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is set to TRUE or at first RRC reconfiguration procedure for UE after switching NRCELL/actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl from TRUE to FALSE   Indicates nominal SRS power for power control. Overrides value configured via User Setup procedure (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_374\_replaced([10974490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U8Mrfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_IF\_389\_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))   L2-PS shall store and use received value as described in 5G\_L2\_19573\_replaced([11146033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24DXYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | CB011123-UPD001 |
| p0NominalPusch | -202...24 | O | Present when NRCELL/actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is set to TRUE or at first RRC reconfiguration procedure for UE after switching NRCELL/actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl from TRUE to FALSE   Indicates nominal UE transmit power for transmission on PUSCH. Overrides value configured via User Setup procedure (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_374\_replaced([10974490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U8Mrfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_IF\_389\_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))   L2-PS shall store and use received value as described in 5G\_L2\_19573\_replaced([11146033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24DXYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | CB011123 |
| targetSinrOffset | -23...23 step 0.1 | O | Present when NRCELL/actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is set to TRUE or at first RRC reconfiguration procedure for UE after switching NRCELL/actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl from TRUE to FALSE but in both cases only when NRCELL/actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to puschSrs or pucchPuschSrs   Indicates offset to the target SINR for PUSCH. Overrides value configured via Cell Setup procedure (see 5G\_L2\_IF\_49\_replaced([10966848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UQ3OPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_IF\_150\_replaced([10969724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UeSoPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))   L2-PS shall store and use received value as described in 5G\_L2\_19573\_replaced([11146033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24DXYvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | CB011123 |
| ForcedTransformPrecoderSwitchInd | ENUM { NotApplicable, success} | M | "NotApplicable" : This indicates that IE “ForcedTransformPrecoderInd” is ignored.   "success" : UE successfully reconfigured to Forced DFT-S-OFDM  per CPRT triggered Forced transform Precoder UE procedure. | CB009849-A |
| slotAggregationInd | ENUM { NotApplicable, success} | M | "NotApplicable" : This indicates that IE “slotAggregationInd” is ignored.   "success" : UE successfully reconfigured to slotAggregation per previously sent message PsUser\_ReconfigurationRequiredInd | CB009849-A |

### 2.4.2.17 DRB Modify

#### 2.4.2.17.0-2 DRB Modify Overview (ID: 10977860)

**2.4.2.17.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10977866`)

DRB Modify
Messages:

PsUser\_DrbModifyReq/PsUser\_DrbModifyResp

Purpose:

To reconfigure UE’s GBR QoS Flow Information L2-PS.

Precondition:

Address distribution is done.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

5G\_L3\_FLOW\_12286: PDU Session Resource Modify [Success] - QoS Flow Addition and/or QoS Flow Deletion and/or QoS Flow Modification, inlcuding 5QI-1 QoS flow

---

#### 2.4.2.17.0-3 DRB Modify Description (ID: 10977872)

**2.4.2.17.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10977878`)

DRB Modify
Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall reconfigure the GBR QoS Flow Information for 5QI-1 bearer(s). Meanwhile, Adaptive Voice TBS of the 5QI-1 bearer(s) shall be reset to initial value, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4914.

---

#### 2.4.2.17.0-4 DRB Modify Message validation (ID: 10977884)

**2.4.2.17.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10977889`)

DRB Modify
Upon reception of the PsUser\_DrbModifyReq message, 5G-L2-PS shall check the validity of the request message.

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_DrbModifyResp message and set the status IE = Ok if the request message is valid and all the requested bearer(s) were setup successfully.

For exception handling, see 5G\_L2\_IF\_557\_replaced([10977895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VPHnPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.17.0-5 DRB Modify Exceptions (ID: 10977895)

**2.4.2.17.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `10977901`)

DRB Modify
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Exception handling rules specifically for object setup can be found in the requirements 5G\_UP\_1805\_replaced([11375008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_1806\_replaced([11375035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueLSqfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_DrbModifyResp message, set the status IE = NotOk, and set cause IE = Undefined, if:

* ueIdDu IE is not known (user does not exist) or;
* crnti IE is not known or;
* one logicalChannelIdentity doesn’t exist, or
* For one logicalChannelIdentity, PsUser\_DrbModifyReq message indicates qosId is 1, but in the 5G-L2-PS UE context corresponding qosId is not 1.

Till now no explicit roll-back mechanism is involved for PsUser\_DrbModifyReq, in the case of failure CP-RT shall presume that no resource has been modified within the 5G-L2-PS.

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of an unexpected exception, 5G-L2-PS shall not send response message.

Error is logged for both expected and unexpected exception.

---

#### 2.4.2.17.1 PsUser_DrbModifyReq

##### 2.4.2.18.1.0-1 Procedures Overview (ID: 10978014)

**2.4.2.18.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10978021`)

Procedures
Messages:

PsUser\_UserChangeInd

Purpose:

To indicate to L2-Ps that state of the UE has changed and the indication doesn't require any type of response or confirmation.

Precondition:

UE context is setup.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

**2.4.2.18.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10978030`)

Procedures
Upon the reception of this message 5G-L2-PS shall store the information about the UE received in the message within the UE context. Each received parameter shall be used later within the respective context.

### 2.4.2.19 Radio Bearer Stop

#### 2.4.2.19.0-2 Radio Bearer Stop Overview (ID: 10978068)

**2.4.2.19.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10978073`)

Radio Bearer Stop
Messages:

PsUser\_BearerStopReq

Direction:

5G-CP-RT -> 5G-L2-PS

Purpose:

This procedure is used to request on ext-DU indirectly through prime-L2-PS to stop scheduling over certain DRB(s) on (one or more) ext-SCell(s), see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11592.

Precondition:

UE context has been setup and inter-gNB CA relation(s) is(are) setup for the relevant SCell(s).

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address in prime-gNB.

Relevant UP Diagram:

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_1694\_replaced([11197985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf94sPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.4.2.19.0-3 Radio Bearer Stop Description (ID: 10978079)

**2.4.2.19.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10978083`)

Radio Bearer Stop
Upon reception of the request, the prime-L2-PS shall follow 5G\_L2\_8581\_replaced([11146074](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24DXaPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.4.2.19.0-4 Radio Bearer Stop Exceptions (ID: 10978087)

**2.4.2.19.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10978092`)

Radio Bearer Stop
Expected Exceptions:

Unexpected Exceptions:

N/A

#### 2.4.2.21 User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication

##### 2.4.2.21.0-2 User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication Overview (ID: 10978160)

**2.4.2.21.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10978165`)

User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication
**Messages:**

[Before CB010741-A] PsUser\_DlBufferMonitoringInd [CB010741-A] PsUser\_BufferMonitoringInd [End CB010741-A]

**Purpose:**

To indicate to 5G-L2-PS DL [CB010741-A] or UL [End CB010741-A] buffer monitoring activation/deactivation notification.

**Precondition:**

UE context is setup.

**Addressing:**

Indication is sent to the PsUser address.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

N/A

---

##### 2.4.2.21.0-3 User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication Description (ID: 10978169)

**2.4.2.21.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12734640`)

User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication
Upon the reception of this message 5G-L2-PS shall store the information about the UE received in the message within the UE context.  5G-L2-PS shall start/stop DL [CB010741-A] or UL [End CB010741-A] buffer monitoring.

---

##### 2.4.2.21.0-4 User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication Exceptions (ID: 10978179)

**2.4.2.21.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10978183`)

User DL/UL Buffer Monitoring Indication
Expected Exceptions:

If the start request from gNB-DU C-Plane is received when the respective monitoring is already running, the request shall be ignored .

If the stop request from gNB-DU C-Plane is received when the respective monitoring is not running, the request shall be ignored .

Unexpected Exceptions:

None.

---

This IE shall be included when one of the value: caActivateDl, caActivateDlAndUl, tputBasedHoActivateDl is included in bufferMonitoring IE. In case of buffer monitoring for Inter-RAT handover purposes dlConfigLevel IE reflects NIDD parameter NRBTS.NRCELL.dlTputBasedIratHoSALevel. [End CB012554-A] |  | CB008311-A |
|  | [Before CB012554-A] dlSCellConfigLevelNum [CB012554-A] dlConfigLevelNum  [End CB012554-A] | 1...200 | O | The number of consecutive subframes that would require [CB012554-A] either [End CB012554-A] CA configuration for serving all the UE non-GBR DL data traffic [CB012554-A] or to trigger inter-RAT handover based on GBR and non-GBR data traffic. [End CB012554-A]  [Before CB012554-A] This IE shall be included when dl or dlAndUl buffer monitoring is activated. [CB012554-A] This IE shall be included when one of the value:  caActivateDl, caActivateDlAndUl, tputBasedHoActivateDl is included in bufferMonitoring IE.  In case of buffer monitoring for Inter-RAT handover purposes dlConfigLevelNum reflects NIDD parameter NRBTS.NRCELL.dlTputBasedIratHoSALevelNum. [End CB012554-A]. |  | CB008311-A |
|  | ulSCellConfigLevel | 1...50 | O | [Before CNI-157588-B] The minimum number of TTIs required to empty the UE's UL non-GBR data buffer in order to trigger SCell addition. [CNI-157588-B] The minimum number of TTIs required to empty the UE's UL non-GBR data buffer to trigger buffer criterion notification. [End CNI-157588-B]  [Before CNI-157588-B] This IE shall be included when  ul or dlAndul buffer monitoring is activated. [CNI-157588-B] This IE shall be included when one of the value: caActivateUl, caActivateDlAndUl is included in bufferMonitoring IE. [End CNI-157588-B] |  | CB010741-A |
|  | ulSCellConfigLevelNum | 1...200 | O | The number of consecutive subframes that would require CA configuration for serving all the UE non-GBR UL data traffic.  [Before CNI-157588] This IE shall be included when ul or dlAndul buffer monitoring is activated. [CNI-157588] This IE shall be included when one of the value: caActivateUl, caActivateDlAndUl is included in bufferMonitoring IE. [End CNI-157588] |  | CB010741-A |
|  | startDlPathloss | Boolean | O | When 5G-CP-RT requests 5G-L2-PS to support DL pathloss consideration for UL CA (see [12774706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_W8ogIIrMEfCrqOdGJPoCRA)), then the parameter shall be present and set to TRUE. Otherwise, the parameter shall be omitted by 5G-CP-RT. At reception, 5G-L2-PS shall proceed according to [11146099](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24DXbPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). |  | CB014587-B |

### 2.4.2.22 User Buffer Criterion Indication

#### 2.4.2.22.0-2 User Buffer Criterion Indication Overview (ID: 10978207)

**2.4.2.22.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10978212`)

User Buffer Criterion Indication
Messages:

PsUser\_BufferCriterionInd

Purpose:

To indicate to C-Plane that the buffer overflow criterion for SCell Addition has been met.

Precondition:

UE context is setup.

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

N/A

---

#### 2.4.2.22.0-3 User Buffer Criterion Indication Description (ID: 10978216)

**2.4.2.22.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12734655`)

User Buffer Criterion Indication
The DL [CB010741-A] or UL [End CB010741-A] buffer overflows and cannot be drained by the serving cell.

[CB010741-A] For DL: [End CB010741-A]

5G-L2-PS shall transmit this indication only when PCell radio link quality checks (see 5G\_L2\_13090\_replaced([11162839](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25ilJ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are passed.

5G-L2-PS stops DL data buffer monitoring and PCell radio link quality monitoring (see 5G\_L2\_13084\_replaced([11162802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25ilIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after this message is sent.

[CB010741-A] For UL:

5G-L2-PS stops UL data buffer monitoring after this message is sent for UL

[End CB010741-A]

---

#### 2.4.2.22.0-4 User Buffer Criterion Indication Exceptions (ID: 10978230)

**2.4.2.22.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12815308`)

User Buffer Criterion Indication
Expected Exceptions:

[CB014587-B]  
Expected Exception 1:

When 5G-L2-PS instance is unable to calculate the dlPathlossDiff parameter due to one of the following conditions:

* The reference DL pathloss value (referenceDlPathloss) is missing or invalid in the related UE context.
* The calculation of the current DL pathloss, based on the PHR from 5G-L2-LO instance, fails, when the buffer criterion for buffer-based SCell Addition is met (criteriaMetDlPathloss).

Then, the 5G-L2-PS instance shall omit the dlPathlossDiff parameter from the message.  
For more details of the calculation handling in 5G-L2-PS, see [13241441](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qYi44MDHEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) for DL Buffer Criterion and [13250983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SbaUgMVgEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) for UL Buffer Criterion.

Expected Exception 2:

When 5G-L2-PS instance is in a DU overload state and receives a request to support DL pathloss consideration for UL CA via PsUser\_BufferMonitoringInd (see [10978187](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VRj2Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then the 5G-L2-PS instance shall ignore the request and omit the dlPathlossDiff parameter from the message.

[End CB014587-B]

Unexpected Exceptions:

None.

---

**2.4.2.22.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `13346101`)

User Buffer Criterion Indication
PsUser\_BufferCriterionInd message content:

| bufferCriterion | [Before CB012554-A] {DL, UL} [CB012554-A] {caDl, caUl, tputBasedHoDl} [End CB012554-A] | M | [Before CB012554-A] DL: buffer criterion for buffer based SCell Addition has been met in the DL. UL:buffer criterion for buffer based SCell Addition has been met in the UL. [CB012554-A] caDl: buffer criterion for CA purposes has been met in DL. caUl: buffer criterion for CA purposes has been met in UL. tputBasedHoDl: buffer criterion for buffer based inter-RAT handover purposes has been met in DL. ### 2.4.2.26 RAN Measurement

#### 2.4.2.26.0-2 RAN Measurement Overview (ID: 10978404)

**2.4.2.26.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10978409`)

RAN Measurement
Messages:

PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq/Resp

Purpose:

To provide various RAN measurements from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT.

Precondition:

UE Context exists.

Addressing:

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

Relevant UP MSCs:

N/A

---

#### 2.4.2.26.0-3 RAN Measurement Description (ID: 10978414)

**2.4.2.26.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `10978430`)

RAN Measurement
The purpose of this message is to provide various gNB RAN measurements from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT

Upon reception of the request, 5G-L2-PS shall verify what kind of measurement was requested and try to collect data needed to create response.

If tAdvMeasRequired IE is set to ‘FALSE’ and angleOfArrivalNrRequired IE is set to ‘FALSE’ and ssbBeamIdRequired IE is set to ‘FALSE’ ,

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_RanMeasurementResp message, set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok and cause IE = ECause5G\_Undefined (see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

tAdvMeasResult IE and angleOfArrivalNrResult IE and ssbBeamIdStatus IE **should be omitted.**

ELSE if requested UE exists

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_RanMeasurementResp message, set the status IE = EStatus5G\_Ok and cause IE = ECause5G\_Undefined (see 5G\_UP\_1846\_replaced([11375790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uePkGPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L2-PS shall obtain the data needed as follows

ELSE

See exceptions in 5G\_L2\_IF\_5732\_replaced([10978444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VTZEPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Initial Timing Advance Measurement:**

If tAdvMeasRequired IE is set to 'TRUE' and requested UE exists:

5G-L2-PS shall try to obtain **[Before CB013507-A] initialTa (Timing Advance Command associated with the PRACH value (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3386, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3387))** [CB013507-A] initialUlEcidTAdv(refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_228\_replaced([11514270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB013507-A] for a requested UE**\*\*\*\*

If current subcellId of a UE is the same as subcellId stored at the reception of PRACH (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3386, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3387):

5G-L2-PS shall fill tAdvMeasResult IE with:

If 5G-L2-PS was able to obtain **[Before CB013507-A] initialTa** [CB013507-A] initialUlEcidTAdv**[End CB013507-A] :**\*\*\*\*

>tAdvStatus IE = Valid

>tAdv IE = value of **[Before CB013507-A] initialTa converted to [Tc] unit as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24666** [CB013507-A] initialUlEcidTAdv**[End CB013507-A]**\*\*\*\*

Else:

>tAdvStatus IE = Invalid\_InitialTaNotAvailable

>tAdv IE should be omitted

Else 5G-L2-PS shall fill tAdvMeasResult IE with:

>tAdvStatus IE = Invalid\_SubcellSwitchDone

>tAdv IE should be omitted

If tAdvMeasRequired IE is set to 'FALSE':

tAdvMeasResult IE should be omitted.

**UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam:**

If angleOfArrivalNrRequired IE is set to 'TRUE' and requested UE exists:

5G-L2-PS shall try to obtain UL Angle of Arrival based on UL beam(5G\_UP\_ALG\_25322) for a requested UE

If dominant UL beam of the UE can be obtained according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25323 **and UL AOA can be determined according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25325:**

5G-L2-PS shall fill angleOfArrivalNrResult IE with:

>aoaNrStatus IE = Valid

>aoaH IE = Horizontal AoA of the determined dominant UL beam(5G\_UP\_ALG\_25325)

>aoaV IE = Vertical AoA of the determined dominant UL beam(5G\_UP\_ALG\_25325).

Else if no dominant beam ID selected according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25323 or UL AOA can not be determined according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25325, 5G-L2-PS shall fill angleOfArrivalNrResult IE with:

>aoaNrStatus IE = Invalid\_noDominantBeam

>aoaH IE should be omitted

>aoaV IE should be omitted

If angleOfArrivalNrRequired IE is set to 'FALSE':

angleOfArrivalNrResult IE should be omitted.

Note: ulAoAMonitorWindow is NIDD parameter received from PsCell\_CellSetupReq/PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq.

If ssbBeamIdRequired IE is set to 'TRUE' and requested UE exists:

5G-L2-PS shall try to obtain UL SSB beam ld (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25920) for a requested UE in case of supercell/subsector.

If valid UL SSB beam Id of the UE can be obtained according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25920 in case of supercell/subsector:

5G-L2-PS shall fill ssbBeamIdResult IE with:

>ssbBeamIdStatus IE = Valid

>ssbBeamId IE = ssb beam Id for UL beam.

Else if SSB beam Id is invalid, 5G-L2-PS shall fill ssbBeamIdResult IE with:

>ssbBeamIdStatus IE = Invalid\_noValidSSB

>ssbBeamId IE should be omitted

If ssbBeamIdRequired IE is set to 'FALSE':

ssbBeamIdResult IE should be omitted.

Note: numOfSuperSubcells/numOfSubSectors are NIDD parameters received from PsCell\_CellSetupReq.

---

#### 2.4.2.26.0-4 RAN Measurement Concurrency handling (ID: 10978435)

**2.4.2.26.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13433711`)

RAN Measurement
[Before CB014535-C] If on demand  UserRanMeasurement procedure is ongoing for UE and 5G-L2-PS receives any other message on PsUser port for the same UE, 5G-L2-PS shall abort ongoing UserRanMeasurement procedure for this UE. [End CB014535-C]

[CB014535-C]   
If periodic UserRanMeasurement procedure is ongoing for UE and 5G-L2-PS receives on demand message on PsUser port for the same UE, 5G-L2-PS shall send immediately on demand PsUser\_RanMeasurementResp with no change in periodic timers and sending periodic PsUser\_RanBundledMeasReportInd.  
[End CB014535-C]

---

#### 2.4.2.26.0-5 RAN Measurement Exceptions (ID: 10978444)

**2.4.2.26.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13408089`)

RAN Measurement
Expected Exceptions:

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_RanMeasurementResp message, set the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause IE = ECause5G\_ObjectDoesNotExist value if (tAdvMeasRequired IE was set to 'TRUE' or angleOfArrivalNrRequired IE was set to 'TRUE' or ssbBeamIdRequired IE was set to 'TRUE') and:

* ueIdDu IE is not known or;
* crnti IE is not known or;
* nrCellIdentity is not known

Optional element tAdvMeasResult should be ommited.

Optional element angleOfArrivalNrResult should be ommited.

Optional element ssbBeamIdResult should be ommited.

[CB014535-B]

5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_RanMeasurementResp ([10978473:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAFPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk and cause IE = ECause5G\_InvalidParameter:

* angleOfArrivalNrRequired =true in PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq ([10978459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAEfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and IE cellTechnology is not TDD FR1 in PsCell\_CellSetupReq ([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* ssbBeamIdRequired = FALSE and tAdvMeasRequired = disabled and ecidPeriodicitySsbAndAccTA is present
* angleOfArrivalNrRequired = FALSE and ecidPeriodicityAoA is present

[Before CB014535-B-UPD003] 5G-L2-PS shall reply with PsUser\_RanMeasurementResp ([10978473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VUAFPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for periodic measurement with the status IE = EStatus5G\_NotOk when PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq is not filled with IE ranMeasAddress. [End CB014535-B-UPD003]

[End CB014535-B]

---

### 2.4.2.27 RAN Measurement Indication

#### 2.4.2.27.0-2 RAN Measurement Indication Overview (ID: 13339149)

**2.4.2.27.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13339150`)

RAN Measurement Indication
**Messages:**

PsUser\_RanBundledMeasReportInd

**Purpose:**

To provide various RAN measurements from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT.

**Precondition:**

UE Context exists and RAN measurements is enabled.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the PsUser address.

The response is sent to the address where the request was sent from.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

N/A

---

#### 2.4.2.27.0-3 RAN Measurement Indication Description (ID: 13339151)

**2.4.2.27.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13339154`)

RAN Measurement Indication
The purpose of this indication is to provide various periodic gNB RAN measurements which are indicated in PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq from 5G-L2-PS to 5G-CP-RT.

---

#### 2.4.2.27.0-4 RAN Measurement Indication Concurrency handling (ID: 13339155)

**2.4.2.27.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13339156`)

RAN Measurement Indication
If PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq procedure is ongoing for UE and 5G-L2-PS receives any other message on PsUser port for the same UE, 5G-L2-PS shall abort ongoing PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq procedure for this UE.

If periodic PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq procedure is ongoing for UE and 5G-L2-PS receives on demand PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq

from 5G-CP-RT for the same UE, 5G-L2-PS shall abort periodic ongoing PsUser\_RanMeasurementReq procedure for this UE.

---

#### 2.4.2.27.0-5 RAN Measurement Indication Exceptions (ID: 13339157)

**2.4.2.27.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13339159`)

RAN Measurement Indication
**Expected Exceptions:**

Generic exception handling rules can be found in the chapter 5G\_UP\_1795\_replaced([11374912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueKrmfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 2.4.2.28 RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication

#### 2.4.2.28.0-1 RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication Overview (ID: 10978493)

**2.4.2.28.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `10978500`)

RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication
Messages:

PsUser\_RrcDeliveryCompletedInd

Purpose:

To indicate to C-Plane the status of RRC message delivery to UE

Precondition:

* LoCtrl\_DlBufferStatusInd with finalRrcDelivery=RrcRelease is received
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31674 specified RRC message delivery procedure is completed

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

* 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_6445\_replaced([11184788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Be4Tg_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Final RRC Delivery

---

#### 2.4.2.28.0-2 RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication Description (ID: 10978505)

**2.4.2.28.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `10978508`)

RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication
When all the HARQ processes containing SRBx (x = 0, 1, 2, 3) are released, L2-PS shall send PsUser\_RrcDeliveryCompletedInd to CP-RT to inform CP-RT that RRC message delivery procedure is completed for all the RRC message SRBs received from higher layer.

---

#### 2.4.2.28.0-3 RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication Exceptions (ID: 10978512)

**2.4.2.28.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `10978516`)

RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication
No exception handling in 5G-L2-PS for PsUser\_RrcDeliveryCompletedInd message. The receiver/client of the message checks the validity where applicable.

Expected Exceptions:

None.

Unexpected Exceptions:

None.

---

#### 2.4.2.28.0-4 RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication PsUser_RrcDeliveryCompletedInd message content (ID: 10978521)

**2.4.2.28.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `10978526`)

RRC Message Delivery Completed Indication
PsUser\_RrcDeliveryCompletedInd message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Range | Optionality | Description | First Feature |
| ueIdDu |  | M | Unique UE Id within gNB-DU. | PR795277 |
| rrcMessageDeliveryStatus | Enum {OK, NOK} | M | This field indicates the general HARQ status for the RRC message transmission. Value ‘OK’ is used when following conditions are all satisfied for all HARQ processes used for RRC message transmission: - when transmission carrying HARQ feedback is not DTX, the CRC check pass and HARQ ACK feedback is received. - Value 'OK' is also used if DTX determined as ACK in the speculative DTX algorithm (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6907). Value ‘NOK’ is used is used when following conditions are all satisfied for any HARQ process used for RRC message transmission: - Transmission carrying HARQ feedback is DTX or CRC check fails or HARQ NACK feedback is received. | PR795277 |

---

### 2.4.2.29 ta exceeded indication

#### 2.4.2.29.0-2 ta exceeded indication Overview (ID: 13255711)

**2.4.2.29.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13255718`)

ta exceeded indication
Message:

PsUser\_TaExceededInd

Purpose:

To indicate to C-Plane that UE has ta >= taDiscThresold

[L2-PS-LEGACY] the message is not supported, 5G-L2-PS shall not send it. [End L2-PS-LEGACY]

Precondition:

* actTaDisconnect feature flag is activated
* UE rrmAccumulatedTimingOffset >= taDiscThreshold for a period of taDiscTimer
* SA call
* FR1 cell

Addressing:

Indication is sent to the PsUser\_UeClient address.

Relevant UP MSCs:

* none

refer to [11150440](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1IfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[L2-PS-LEGACY] the message is not supported, 5G-L2-PS shall not send it. [End L2-PS-LEGACY]

### 2.4.2.30 Reserve CFRA Preamble Request

#### 2.4.2.30.0-2 Reserve CFRA Preamble Request Overview (ID: 13426460)

**2.4.2.30.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13392315`)

Reserve CFRA Preamble Request
**Messages:**

PsUser\_ReserveCfraPreambleReq

PsUser\_ReserveCfraPreambleResp

**Purpose:**

To request CPRT assign preamble from configured CFRA pool, which will be used in PDCCH Order procedure for timing alignment of non collocated SCell (with different TAG Id, see [13345951: Timing Alignment via CFRA](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_L_qpQOSSEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ)).

**Precondition:**

SCell was activated and PCell requested SCell to perform timing alignment.

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the CP-RT address.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

[13415683: Timing Alignment procedure for SCell in different TAG](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_GHt_khPTEfG3gf_qmG8Vww)

---

#### 2.4.2.30.0-3 Reserve CFRA Preamble Request Description (ID: 13426601)

**2.4.2.30.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13392322`)

Reserve CFRA Preamble Request
1. L2-PS requests CP-RT to assign a preamble from CFRA pool for given SSB beam.
2. CP-RT checks if there is available CFRA preamble and returns withing response message.
3. L2-PS uses this preamble to order Random Access procedure as part of timing alignment procedure. As long as preamble is reserved it can't be used in other procedures like Handover.

---

#### 2.4.2.30.0-4 Reserve CFRA Preamble Request Exceptions (ID: 13426607)

**2.4.2.30.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13392327`)

Reserve CFRA Preamble Request
Expected Exceptions:

* in case of any problem with obtaining preamble CP-RT will respond with failure.

Unexpeced Exceptions:

* none

---

#### 2.4.2.30.0-5 Reserve CFRA Preamble Request PsUser_ReserveCfraPreambleReq (ID: 13426635)

**2.4.2.30.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13382566`)

Reserve CFRA Preamble Request
PsUser\_ReserveCfraPreambleReq message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Optionality** | **Description** | **First Feature** |
| nrCellIdentity | 0...2^36-1 | M | cell ID, unique within PLMN | CB015279-A |
| ueIdDu | 0…2^32-1 | M | Unique UE Id within gNB-DU. | CB015279-A |
| ssbBeamId | 0..7 | M | Defines for which SSB beam CFRA preamble is requested. For non-beamforming configuration value is defaulted to 0. | CB015279-A |
| reservationTime | 0..20000 | M | Longest time in ms L2-PS will need preamble to be able to finish CFRA procedure. | CB015279-A |

---

**2.4.2.31.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13392331`)

Release CFRA Preamble Indication
L2-PS indicates CFRA preamble is no longer needed by L2-PS (either successful or failed timing alignment procedure), CP-RT no longer considers preamble reserved and allows it to be used for other purposes.

| timeStamp | [timeStamp](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kToY8tBFEfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) | O | Periodic and on demand time stamp for tA and accTA when [Before CB014535-SR-A-UPD002] the measurement is collected before sending in PsUser\_RanBundledMeasReportInd. [CB014535-SR-A-UPD002] the measurement happened so when any of the following is received for the UE \* PRACH reception SFN, slot \* PUSCH reception SFN, slot (which is used for computing rrmUeLongTermPuschTimingOffset) \* PUCCH F3  reception SFN, slot (which is used for computing rrmUeLongTermPucchTimingOffset) [End CB014535-SR-A-UPD002] IE is provided if tAdvStatus is valid. |  | CB014535-B |
| relativeTime | BIT STRING (SIZE (64)) | O | Periodic and on demand relativeTime for tA and accTA when the measurement happened so when any of the following is received for the UE \* PRACH reception SFN, slot \* PUSCH reception SFN, slot (which is used for computing rrmUeLongTermPuschTimingOffset) \* PUCCH F3  reception SFN, slot (which is used for computing rrmUeLongTermPucchTimingOffset) The IE represents Time in seconds relative to 00:00:00 on 1 January 1970. IE is provided if tAdvStatus is valid. |  | CB014535-SR-A-UPD002 |

---
